```python
'''
Manages Job Queues for Asynchronous Processing
'''
from queue import Queue
class JobQueue:
    def __init__(self):
        self.queue = Queue()
    def add_job(self, job):
        # Logic to add job to queue
        self.queue.put(job)
        print("Job added to queue.")
    def process_jobs(self):
        while not self.queue.empty():
            job = self.queue.get()
            print(f"Processing job: {job}")
            # Execute job logic here
            self.queue.task_done()
```

pii_handler.py
```python
'''
Secure Handling of Personally Identifiable Information (PII)
'''
from cryptography.fernet import Fernet
class PIIHandler:
    def __init__(self):
        self.key = Fernet.generate_key()
        self.cipher_suite = Fernet(self.key)
    def secure_data(self, data):
        # Logic to secure PII
        encrypted_data = self.cipher_suite.encrypt(data.encode())
        print("PII secured.")
        return encrypted_data
    def retrieve_data(self, encrypted_data):
        decrypted_data = self.cipher_suite.decrypt(encrypted_data).decode()
        print("PII retrieved.")
        return decrypted_data
```
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)
```

# B2B SaaS MVP User Manual

Welcome to the B2B SaaS MVP user manual. This document will guide you through the installation, setup, and usage of our software, which automates dispute evidence collection, generates indexed watermarked/redacted PDFs, interfaces with Stripe and PayPal APIs, integrates with Shopify, and incorporates job queues with secure handling of Personally Identifiable Information (PII).

## Table of Contents

1. [Introduction](#introduction)
2. [Main Features](#main-features)
3. [Installation](#installation)
4. [Usage](#usage)
5. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)
6. [Support](#support)

## Introduction

This B2B SaaS MVP is designed to streamline the process of handling disputes by automating evidence collection, generating secure PDFs, and integrating with popular payment and e-commerce platforms. It is built using Python and leverages several libraries to provide a comprehensive solution for businesses.

## Main Features

- **Automated Dispute Evidence Collection**: Collects evidence from specified APIs to support dispute resolution.
- **PDF Generation**: Creates indexed, watermarked, and redacted PDFs using Pyppeteer2.
- **Payment Integration**: Interfaces with Stripe and PayPal APIs to process payments.
- **Shopify Integration**: Connects with Shopify to manage e-commerce operations.
- **Job Queue Management**: Handles asynchronous processing of tasks.
- **Secure PII Handling**: Encrypts and decrypts personally identifiable information to ensure data security.

## Installation

### Prerequisites

- Python 3.8 or higher
- pip (Python package installer)

### Steps

1. **Clone the Repository**:
   ```bash
   git clone <repository-url>
   cd <repository-directory>
   ```

2. **Install Dependencies**:
   Use the following command to install all required dependencies:
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. **Configure API Keys**:
   - Update `payment_integration.py` with your Stripe and PayPal API keys.
   - Update `shopify_integration.py` with your Shopify API credentials.

## Usage

1. **Run the Application**:
   Execute the main application script to start the GUI:
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

2. **Using the GUI**:
   - **Collect Evidence**: Click the "Collect Evidence" button to initiate evidence collection.
   - **Generate PDF**: Click the "Generate PDF" button to create a PDF document.
   - **Quit**: Click the "QUIT" button to exit the application.

3. **Processing Payments**:
   - Payments can be processed through the integrated Stripe and PayPal APIs by providing the necessary payment data.

4. **Shopify Integration**:
   - Ensure your Shopify credentials are correctly configured to connect and manage your Shopify store.

## Troubleshooting

- **Dependency Issues**: Ensure all dependencies are installed correctly by checking the `requirements.txt` file.
- **API Connectivity**: Verify that API keys and credentials are correctly configured and that there is an active internet connection.
- **PDF Generation Errors**: Ensure Pyppeteer2 is correctly installed and configured.

## Support

For further assistance, please contact our support team at [support@chatdev.com](mailto:support@chatdev.com).

Thank you for choosing our B2B SaaS MVP. We hope it enhances your business operations and dispute resolution processes.
